  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0a79940f-30e4-47e3-ac92-010757b736a7'
      });

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6339443865303406146">I was on pins and needles for ages waiting for this book, biting nails, stalking LB- I was dying for more of Slade and Mercy after book 2 left me utterly unable to form coherent words/thoughts other than FUCK.<br/>I loved parts of this book and some of it made me insane..... Maybe my expectations were too high because I wanted it so damn bad BUT...<br/>I was a little disappointed. <br/>While I loved the book and, OMG! LB can write some hot as sin, keep me wet, panting and horny as hell sex scenes, it fell a li</span>
  <span id="freeText6339443865303406146" style="display:none">I was on pins and needles for ages waiting for this book, biting nails, stalking LB- I was dying for more of Slade and Mercy after book 2 left me utterly unable to form coherent words/thoughts other than FUCK.<br />I loved parts of this book and some of it made me insane..... Maybe my expectations were too high because I wanted it so damn bad BUT...<br />I was a little disappointed. <br />While I loved the book and, OMG! LB can write some hot as sin, keep me wet, panting and horny as hell sex scenes, it fell a little short for me. The last 15-20% of this book is what I wish at least 50% was about. <br />Slade and Mercy have some serious fucked up issues....ESPECIALLY Slade and we have watched them overcome so much as this trilogy progressed. Slade, being the sadistic, masochist that he is, got totally consumed with his darkness and I wish there was a little less 'fix Slade" and a lot more 'torture Abraham".<br />Although I am a tiny bit disappointed, I absolutely LOVE Slade and Mercy and all of their fuckedupness! <br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1367490995" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1367490995" />
    <a title="Hilary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28678670-hilary"><img alt="Hilary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440364894p2/28678670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1367490995?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hilary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hilary" href="/user/show/28678670-hilary">Hilary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26123136-beg-for-mercy">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1367490995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1331105275885195503">Beg for Mercy is everything I hoped for and more. It’s not just a 3rd book in a series -- It has its own heart. Its own signature that will stay with you long after you read “The End.” A Holy-Crazy Batman roller-coaster ride of emotional twists and turns that will leave you gasping.<br/> <br/>This book is raw, angsty and emotional. We see a new side of all of the characters. The self doubts and struggles I have been waiting for all along finally come out to play, making this my favorite book in the series</span>
  <span id="freeText1331105275885195503" style="display:none">Beg for Mercy is everything I hoped for and more. It’s not just a 3rd book in a series -- It has its own heart. Its own signature that will stay with you long after you read “The End.” A Holy-Crazy Batman roller-coaster ride of emotional twists and turns that will leave you gasping.<br /> <br />This book is raw, angsty and emotional. We see a new side of all of the characters. The self doubts and struggles I have been waiting for all along finally come out to play, making this my favorite book in the series. I can’t even begin to describe the myriad of emotions I felt while reading this masterpiece- anger, heartache, disgust, elation, relief.<br /> <br />Lucian shows us brilliant, three- dimensional characters that, even if you aren’t familiar with their demons, you feel like you can relate to them. He magically weaves a dark tale with the bright light of hope, showing that love and light can conquer your demons. His strategic placement of humor has you choking out a laugh even amidst the nail biting action and gut wrenching tears.<br /> <br />5 Beautifully Broken, Glued together and now, Shiny and New Stars for this magnificent book!<br /> <br />** I had received a review copy in exchange for an honest review. Reviewed on behalf of Bookalicious Babes Blog **</span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369413169" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12299505177740242436">5 Amazing Dark Intense Thrilling Stars! <br/>I’m at a loss for words…. Okay regrouping. Wow what a book. First off I have to say Lucian you did an absolutely amazing job with this series. Each book in this series just kept getting better and better. <br/><a href='http://s1102.photobucket.com/user/Novachick1213/media/BKzLu_zpsiyc15xwv.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/>Usually in most series the reader can predict what’s going to happen by the third book but not the case with the series. There were so many great twist and turns throughout this book you’ll have not clue which way is up. Just when you thing everything</span>
  <span id="freeText12299505177740242436" style="display:none">5 Amazing Dark Intense Thrilling Stars! <br>I’m at a loss for words…. Okay regrouping. Wow what a book. First off I have to say Lucian you did an absolutely amazing job with this series. Each book in this series just kept getting better and better. <br><a href="http://s1102.photobucket.com/user/Novachick1213/media/BKzLu_zpsiyc15xwv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440111171ra/15931114.gif" alt=" photo BKzLu_zpsiyc15xwv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Usually in most series the reader can predict what’s going to happen by the third book but not the case with the series. There were so many great twist and turns throughout this book you’ll have not clue which way is up. Just when you thing everything’s over BOOM something else pops right up. So with that being said I am so sad to see this story come to an end. It was one awesome journey. <br>I though Mercy and No Mercy bought out every single emotion I thought I had but Beg for Mercy O.M.G. I went through an entire box of tissues while reading this book. I cried, I laughed, I cursed and I cried some more. By the end of the book I was one big old ball of snot and tears.<br><a href="http://s1102.photobucket.com/user/Novachick1213/media/giphy_zpstywytq91.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440111171ra/15931115.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpstywytq91.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Beg for Mercy starts off at full speed right from the very first page and doesn’t slow down until the very last word of the book. Right out of the gates we see Sade and Mercy fighting to make their relationship work. This was just so emotional, at times it felt like I was right there going through everything with them. Watching Sade come to terms with and work on controlling his sadomasochist demons is wow! Oh and we also get to a little softer side to Mercy which was great (but she’s still tough as nails). For me personally this made Mercy a little more real in my opinion. Will love concur all? I’m not saying. My lips are sealed. Are all the loss end’s tied up? How yes how you ask? Go read the book to find out!<br><a href="http://s1102.photobucket.com/user/Novachick1213/media/tumblr_inline_nhct1uouPv1qjw76h_zpsazi1an7o.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423177671ra/13595577.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_nhct1uouPv1qjw76h_zpsazi1an7o.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3167667542739719451">Wow! Where to start?!<br/>Lucian Bane once again sets us down, with our nervous quivering tummies and straps us in that wonderful rollercoaster... Only hold on tight because this one goes where your least expecting! Keep all hands in feet inside the car at all times!!! Dont allow yourself to be fooled by those calm swaying hills and let your guard down! And i promise, when you get off your legs will be knocking knees and the snotty tears are rolling off your cheeks while you smile at the same time! W</span>
  <span id="freeText3167667542739719451" style="display:none">Wow! Where to start?!<br />Lucian Bane once again sets us down, with our nervous quivering tummies and straps us in that wonderful rollercoaster... Only hold on tight because this one goes where your least expecting! Keep all hands in feet inside the car at all times!!! Dont allow yourself to be fooled by those calm swaying hills and let your guard down! And i promise, when you get off your legs will be knocking knees and the snotty tears are rolling off your cheeks while you smile at the same time! We are talking about Bane, after all...<br /><br />The conclusion of Sade and Mercy will have you laughing, crying, wanting to puke your guts up and then asking Lucian Bane to do it all over again by the very end!<br />The thing I loved most was that, I felt, not only do we see Sade heal...we see Mercy heal, which I must admit, I was not expecting. With the emotions, the action, the suspense, the love and just the right amount of darkness thrown in ...All I can say is 'Expect the unexpected!'</span>

<div id="review_1356995234" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1356995234" />
    <a title="Hilary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28678670-hilary"><img alt="Hilary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440364894p2/28678670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1356995234?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hilary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hilary" href="/user/show/28678670-hilary">Hilary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1356995234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4512644406572659989">Beg for Mercy is everything I hoped for and more. It’s not just a 3rd book in a series -- It has its own heart. Its own signature that will stay with you long after you read “The End.” A Holy-Crazy Batman roller-coaster ride of emotional twists and turns that will leave you gasping.<br/><br/>This book is raw, angsty and emotional. We see a new side of all of the characters. The self doubts and struggles I have been waiting for all along finally come out to play, making this my favorite book in the series.</span>
  <span id="freeText4512644406572659989" style="display:none">Beg for Mercy is everything I hoped for and more. It’s not just a 3rd book in a series -- It has its own heart. Its own signature that will stay with you long after you read “The End.” A Holy-Crazy Batman roller-coaster ride of emotional twists and turns that will leave you gasping.<br /><br />This book is raw, angsty and emotional. We see a new side of all of the characters. The self doubts and struggles I have been waiting for all along finally come out to play, making this my favorite book in the series. I can’t even begin to describe the myriad of emotions I felt while reading this masterpiece- anger, heartache, disgust, elation, relief.<br /><br />Lucian shows us brilliant, three- dimensional characters that, even if you aren’t familiar with their demons, you feel like you can relate to them. He magically weaves a dark tale with the bright light of hope, showing that love and light can conquer your demons. His strategic placement of humor has you choking out a laugh even amidst the nail biting action and gut wrenching tears.<br /><br />5 Beautifully Broken, Glued together and now, Shiny and New Stars for this magnificent book!<br /><br />** I had received a review copy in exchange for an honest review. Reviewed on behalf of Bookalicious Babes Blog **</span>
  <a data-text-id="4512644406572659989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14490965552737459397" style="display:none">Holy freaking hell! Seriously?? OK, yes I devoured this book...waiting and wanting and BEGGING for it to go live, I was NOT disappointed!! Lucian Bane has a way of sucking you into this world and loosing your sense of reality while your engrossed in the pain and pleasure of this series. <br /><br />Mercy and Sade are an explosive couple and utterly compliment and push each other like no other characters I have EVER read. I was enthralled and entranced into their therapy and love and devastatingly beautiful relationship. Their love is one that shows no matter what demons you face there are worse things out there and they lurk right around the corners. With help of family and friends this story is EPIC!! I can't even express to you the depths of emotions that pour off the pages and had me gasping with tears running down my cheeks trying to finish some scenes. And yes some moments on wanting to smack the bajesus out of Sade and Mercy alike. LOL But I loved it all, all the thought, love, pain, and utter joy of it. <br /><br />I can't recommend this series and this author enough. EVERY time I pick up a book I know I am going to get a good story and FEEL something. And this didn't have anything lacking! Perfect compliment to the series and can't wait to see what comes next! #oneclick #begforit #Mercy</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2111060622510402022">Simply amazing and so good<br/><br/>This is the third book in the series - you'll need to read the others first. This book needs more than five stars.   <span id="freeText2111060622510402022" style="display:none">Simply amazing and so good<br /><br />This is the third book in the series - you'll need to read the others first. This book needs more than five stars. I loved it and couldn't get enough, I was hooked. The raw emotions that you will feel in this book, yes it's real. This book will stick with you and touch a special place in your heart. To feel the connection between Sade and Mercy, makes you know you are truly connected in the book. <br /><br />In this book, you will find out what happens. All your questions will be answered, thou be prepared for an emotional read. You'll be hooked in the beginning and need to finish. <br /><br />Mercy &amp; Sade have a hard battle for them both. They have issues and pasts that are dark, that will need helped forgetting and accepting new. Having Father Abraham still coming for them keeps them focused on battles.Can love help them? Can forgiveness help? You'll get those answers. <br /><br />A very amazing story to end the series. This book and series is one of my favorites this year. A truly heartfelt story that will stick with you. Great job Lucian. </span>

<div id="review_1356271870" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1356271870" />
    <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews"><img alt="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464483219p2/12941902.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1356271870?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="user" itemprop="url" name="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews">RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1356271870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13642060159059935576">We all have demons, some of us are able to control it and others let it control them. We tend to give them the power to tell us if we are capable of loving others and if we are worthy of love in return. <br/><br/>In this installment Sade is struggling with his past interfering with his present and he is losing all hope for the future. He feels he needs to protect Mercy from this beast inside of him and the only way to do that is by letting her go, pushing her away. Meanwhile, Mercy has made her mind up to</span>
  <span id="freeText13642060159059935576" style="display:none">We all have demons, some of us are able to control it and others let it control them. We tend to give them the power to tell us if we are capable of loving others and if we are worthy of love in return. <br /><br />In this installment Sade is struggling with his past interfering with his present and he is losing all hope for the future. He feels he needs to protect Mercy from this beast inside of him and the only way to do that is by letting her go, pushing her away. Meanwhile, Mercy has made her mind up to fight for the man she loves, the man she knows is deep inside of Sade. She is holding on tight to him and no amount of pushing is loosening that grip. <br /><br />This conclusion to Sade &amp; Mercy's journey will drag you through every emotion you can imagine. There were moments where Sade was vulnerable and my heart broke in two, only to be laughing a few minutes later and then ready to throw my Ipad in the next. The constant push and pull was exhausting, maddening and invigorating all at once. I often found myself expecting them to give up, thinking they were beyond help and then cheering them on and celebrating their successes. There were a couple of scenes that will resonate with mothers, it will break your heart and leave you gasping for air. I was literally clutching my chest and trying to keep the tears in and then later I was fist pumping and screaming "Hell yes!". <br /><br />I really enjoyed Sade's character in this book, we were able to see him raw, exposed and vulnerable. You could literally feel the turmoil he was going through and the inner struggle with that beast within. Mercy's character was hit or miss at times until you see that she is struggling with her own demons and just trying to break through to Sade by any means necessary. She may appear to be pushy, whiny and weak in some places but she is resilient, strong and she is fighting a battle that is outside of her comfort zone. <br /><br />The scenes were hot, the story flowed well, there were twists in there that I didn't expect and the author placed humorous, light-hearted scenes in the story at the appropriate times to give you an emotional reprieve. I felt like most of the scenes were realistically portrayed with normal reactions to those scenarios which you don't always find in the fictional world. <br /><br />As always, my favorite quotes <br /><br />"Why would God ...his voice trembled out with several gasps, "send me...an angel?" He turned to her, so confused, his bloodshot eyes, pleading for answers. "Do you think...." his voice barely whispered now, "that maybe....He made a mistake?" ~Sade <br /><br />"I fucking want to do things Mercy. I want your pleasure, but God, I want your fucking pain." ~Sade <br /><br />"You get pleasure from pain...," "And I'm going to teach you how to get pain...from my pleasure." ~Mercy<br /><br />Relentlessbookchic approved &amp; recommended </span>
  <a data-text-id="13642060159059935576" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1357018506" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1357018506" />
    <a title="Barbara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25523602-barbara"><img alt="Barbara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498085104p2/25523602.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1357018506?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Barbara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Barbara" href="/user/show/25523602-barbara">Barbara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25523602-barbara?shelf=erotic-thriller">erotic-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1357018506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7300485192677417922">Beg for Mercy is the powerful conclusion to The Mercy Series: Mercy & No Mercy. It is a wrap up of all the dangling parts in the first two books and it was done with the precision of a surgeon with a scalpel, because that is just how good Lucian Bane’s writing is.<br/><br/>My emotions were all over the place in this book. The conversation between Sade and his Mom about the unspeakable sexual abusive he suffered as a child was beyond heartbreaking, cried my eyes out. Then you have Mercy, smart, tough, beau</span>
  <span id="freeText7300485192677417922" style="display:none">Beg for Mercy is the powerful conclusion to The Mercy Series: Mercy &amp; No Mercy. It is a wrap up of all the dangling parts in the first two books and it was done with the precision of a surgeon with a scalpel, because that is just how good Lucian Bane’s writing is.<br /><br />My emotions were all over the place in this book. The conversation between Sade and his Mom about the unspeakable sexual abusive he suffered as a child was beyond heartbreaking, cried my eyes out. Then you have Mercy, smart, tough, beautiful and so in love with Sade. Her obsession with helping him rid his demons before they break them apart was unrelenting. The passion and the strength that ensued in their endeavor to work thru these problems was heartbreaking at times. But then there was the sex, which was hot, dirty, erotic and out of control which took my breath away!! <br /><br />Then there was Kane, who is lethal, charming and in command of all things, all of the time. OMG, I love this character. He is everything you should fear but instead admire because of his strength and his steadfastness to take care of those he loved. His handling of Abraham was a thing of beauty. I was cheering with every horrible thing he wanted to do to him. <br /><br />I loved the ending of this book!! It blew my mind because I wasn’t expecting it and I’m smiling now thinking about how beautiful it was. This book certainly had its dark side but then there was the light, and when it came out it shined like the most beautiful crystal clear sunny day that you have ever seen!! Thank you Lucian, for giving us an epic ending to a truly unforgettable series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7300485192677417922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6872856020882488579"><br/>My Review of Beg For Mercy By: Lucian Bane<br/>My Rating 5 Bravo Stars<br/>The conclusion of this series, Lucian pulled no punches with this story, I thought the angst and frustration I felt in the last two books could not be topped, Oh how wrong was I. I underestimated the power of this amazing author his writing is brilliant the way he sucks you in and makes you become a part of the story. What an emotional journey this book was.   <span id="freeText6872856020882488579" style="display:none"><br />My Review of Beg For Mercy By: Lucian Bane<br />My Rating 5 Bravo Stars<br />The conclusion of this series, Lucian pulled no punches with this story, I thought the angst and frustration I felt in the last two books could not be topped, Oh how wrong was I. I underestimated the power of this amazing author his writing is brilliant the way he sucks you in and makes you become a part of the story. What an emotional journey this book was. It has left me with a book handover.<br />Mercy is the most incredible woman, and Sade is such a tormented man. The substance you absorb while reading their story has a pleasure- pain element you can’t imagine not having. This book keeps you dangling on the edge, hoping that Sade’s demons can be Mercified. There was a twist in the story I never saw coming and it blew me away. I won’t give away any spoilers you must read for yourself. I highly recommend this series. This series is now in my Top 5 Best Reads. One Click yours today.<br />*Reviewed for Hellmouth’s Bookblog &amp; Reviews*<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4485633746485108653"><strong>Simply amazing and so good</strong><br/><br/>This is the third book in the series - you'll need to read the others first.   <span id="freeText4485633746485108653" style="display:none"><strong>Simply amazing and so good</strong><br /><br />This is the third book in the series - you'll need to read the others first. This book needs more than five stars. I loved it and couldn't get enough, I was hooked. The raw emotions that you will feel in this book, yes it's real. This book will stick with you and touch a special place in your heart. To feel the connection between Sade and Mercy, makes you know you are truly connected in the book. <br /><br />In this book, you will find out what happens. All your questions will be answered, thou be prepared for an emotional read. You'll be hooked in the beginning and need to finish. <br /><br />Mercy &amp; Sade have a hard battle for them both. They have issues and pasts that are dark, that will need helped forgetting and accepting new. Having Father Abraham still coming for them keeps them focused on battles.Can love help them? Can forgiveness help? You'll get those answers. <br /><br />A very amazing story to end the series. This book and series is one of my favorites this year. A truly heartfelt story that will stick with you. Great job Lucian. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10492642841577708500"><br/>********Spoiler Alert*******<br/><br/><br/>Storytelling at its BEST! Mr. Bane's BOOM gets BETTER & BETTER..<br/><br/>I have been looking forward to the next book in this series. This being the conclusion, leaves me a little sad and with a major book hang-over!<br/>This is not my usual kind of read, but I am so glad that I took a chance on this story and the author. Most of us fight one kind of demon or another, and it's good to see the characters in this story finally catch a break. That they fight for each other and win and</span>
  <span id="freeText10492642841577708500" style="display:none"><br />********Spoiler Alert*******<br /><br /><br />Storytelling at its BEST! Mr. Bane's BOOM gets BETTER &amp; BETTER..<br /><br />I have been looking forward to the next book in this series. This being the conclusion, leaves me a little sad and with a major book hang-over!<br />This is not my usual kind of read, but I am so glad that I took a chance on this story and the author. Most of us fight one kind of demon or another, and it's good to see the characters in this story finally catch a break. That they fight for each other and win and even find that HEA! The writer tells the story in vivid &amp; rich detail, that sets you right in the room with the characters as the story goes!<br />White knuckle, stomach sinking, heart pounding,wonderfully funny just where you need it most,sizzling hot &amp; most of all hopeful. The story of overcoming the odds, family, twists, thrilling suspense, soul meshing and emotional. A strong cast and the hero and the heroine lead the way all the way to the tearful ending. Leaving the conclusion of this trilogy branded on your heart for all time. Mr. Bane grows as a story teller and writer with each new book. You're like "NO HE DIDN'T'- OMG YES HE DID! He puts a spell on your brain heart and soul. And always leaves you with a BOOK HANGOVER that many writers cannot compare to. This author and this dark series are at the top of my list. Leaving the reader with hope for better days, that demons can at least be controlled if not overcome and that most all deserve a second chance with love and hope!<br /> A MUST READ!!!!<br /></span>

    <a title="Jen Cothran" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18790454-jen-cothran"><img alt="Jen Cothran" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467163370p2/18790454.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1360968138?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Cothran" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Cothran" href="/user/show/18790454-jen-cothran">Jen Cothran</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=thc-reading-challenge">thc-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=one-click-worthy">one-click-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=bondage">bondage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18790454-jen-cothran?shelf=dominance">dominance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1360968138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11073949135247402404">Holy freaking hell! Seriously?? OK, yes I devoured this book...waiting and wanting and BEGGING for it to go live, I was NOT disappointed!! Lucian Bane has a way of sucking you into this world and loosing your sense of reality while your engrossed in the pain and pleasure of this series. <br/><br/>Mercy and Sade are an explosive couple and utterly compliment and push each other like no other characters I have EVER read. I was enthralled and entranced into their therapy and love and devastatingly beautiful </span>
  <span id="freeText11073949135247402404" style="display:none">Holy freaking hell! Seriously?? OK, yes I devoured this book...waiting and wanting and BEGGING for it to go live, I was NOT disappointed!! Lucian Bane has a way of sucking you into this world and loosing your sense of reality while your engrossed in the pain and pleasure of this series. <br /><br />Mercy and Sade are an explosive couple and utterly compliment and push each other like no other characters I have EVER read. I was enthralled and entranced into their therapy and love and devastatingly beautiful relationship. Their love is one that shows no matter what demons you face there are worse things out there and they lurk right around the corners. With help of family and friends this story is EPIC!! I can't even express to you the depths of emotions that pour off the pages and had me gasping with tears running down my cheeks trying to finish some scenes. And yes some moments on wanting to smack the bajesus out of Sade and Mercy alike. LOL But I loved it all, all the thought, love, pain, and utter joy of it. <br /><br />I can't recommend this series and this author enough. EVERY time I pick up a book I know I am going to get a good story and FEEL something. And this didn't have anything lacking! Perfect compliment to the series and can't wait to see what comes next! #oneclick #begforit #Mercy </span>
  <a data-text-id="11073949135247402404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1368782053?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          added it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1368782053" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11348625096184282039"><strong>The beautiful end to one crazy series!</strong><br/><br/>Few words can express how much I enjoyed this series. Each book that was read brought out so many emotion. There were tears, laughter, anxiety, anticipation, and at times growling at the characters. But the story of Sade and Mercy is one train ride that should not be missed. Two broken souls. Fighting their pasts. Fighting for healing. Fighting for love.<br/><br/>" Love. It’s what Mercy desperately needed from him. And it’s what he didn’t have to give. Not the kind sh</span>
  <span id="freeText11348625096184282039" style="display:none"><strong>The beautiful end to one crazy series!</strong><br /><br />Few words can express how much I enjoyed this series. Each book that was read brought out so many emotion. There were tears, laughter, anxiety, anticipation, and at times growling at the characters. But the story of Sade and Mercy is one train ride that should not be missed. Two broken souls. Fighting their pasts. Fighting for healing. Fighting for love.<br /><br />" Love. It’s what Mercy desperately needed from him. And it’s what he didn’t have to give. Not the kind she deserved. All he had was a mind and body twisted and tangled with the cruelty of his life."<br /><br />To fulfill the emptiness in their souls they hold tight to each other. But with the revelations that have come to pass, demons are bound to surface. Clawing and breaking down those well built walls. And as Sade give way to what he knows, Mercy is fighting to bring him back. But nothing worth fighting for is ever easy.<br /><br />" That fucking look had encased his heart like a hot silk, caressing, promising, calling him out in ways that confused his mind. The contradiction was enough to break his fury long enough for him to let go."<br /><br />I am so emotionally exhausted. But every page was oh so worth it. To bring such a strong message thru this story is breathtaking. The past can only take hold of what we allow it to. Love can conquer all. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11348625096184282039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6945102657503910402">Beautifully written, I was drawn in, turning page after page, wanting to know how this story would reach its conclusion. I was not disappointed! There where times as I was reading this that my heart was in my throat. The raw emotions I felt with these characters was unleashed with an amazing feeling of empathy.   <span id="freeText6945102657503910402" style="display:none">Beautifully written, I was drawn in, turning page after page, wanting to know how this story would reach its conclusion. I was not disappointed! There where times as I was reading this that my heart was in my throat. The raw emotions I felt with these characters was unleashed with an amazing feeling of empathy. Some of us have been in the darkness, we know how that feels and when we discover that light, it's a feeling of pure exhilaration. This book was not only a fabulous read but I learned something that has been with me for years. With darkness there is light. We fight our demons and if we have faith and patience we will overcome. These two beautiful tortured souls came out of hell to find what they needed to be free of their past. What an excellent ending! I Loved it all!<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3784267296048198857">I loved the final book in the Mercy Trilogy!<br/><br/>Sade finally fights his demons, but not without a butt-whooping. Mercy embraces the role of Sade's therapist and boy do sparks fly!<br/><br/>Lucian Bane explores the depth of his characters' lives and gives us a glimps of how difficult Sade really had it at the hands of his cruel, paedophile father.<br/><br/>Sade embraces his new-found second chance with his mother and Mercy's dad. With the help of Mercy, he learns to accept love.<br/><br/>It is a great love story. I couldn't think</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kimberly Caldwell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kimberly Caldwell" href="/user/show/12580891-kimberly-caldwell">Kimberly Caldwell</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1366180489" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13523198991555311143">Wow. I don't know any other way to put my awe at this book. The wait for its release was torturous, and I drank down every single word as I read it. The final installment in this series was well worth the wait.<br/><br/>I am not an eloquent writer, so I can't sum up this story as well as some of my fellow Lucian Bane fans can. But I can tell you that I am absolutely and completely in love with Sade and Mercy. This story tugged at so many strings in me. It called to parts of me I didn't know existed. In an</span>
  <span id="freeText13523198991555311143" style="display:none">Wow. I don't know any other way to put my awe at this book. The wait for its release was torturous, and I drank down every single word as I read it. The final installment in this series was well worth the wait.<br /><br />I am not an eloquent writer, so I can't sum up this story as well as some of my fellow Lucian Bane fans can. But I can tell you that I am absolutely and completely in love with Sade and Mercy. This story tugged at so many strings in me. It called to parts of me I didn't know existed. In an age when so many authors are putting out books that touch on the world of BDSM, and a good portion of those not knowing much, or anything, about the lifestyle, it's refreshing to read something written by someone who knows what they are talking about. Someone who understands the emotions behind the characters, and can pull the reader in to experience those emotions right along with them. I felt like I was on a roller coaster for this entire series, but most especially this last book. The highest of the highs and lowest of the lows.<br /><br />I cannot recommend this entire series enough. This will forever be one of my Top 10 books/series. Congratulations, Luc, on another FANTASTIC release!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13523198991555311143" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

They were both mistreated as children and brought together as adults so that they could heal each other. I was truly ecstatic that the author made sure that fate and justice were served in the end. This is a strong story and the subject matter is not for everyone. But if you give it a try I believe you will get hooked just as I did.</span>

  <span id="freeText6931941509312100752" style="display:none">I've been hooked on this series since the first page of Mercy. Lucian Bane has this way of weaving a web of twisted love that you never ever want to get out of.<br /><br />I've been anxious for this conclusion since I closed No Mercy months ago and it does not disappoint.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ufn9F4pMPxL64s1y/8VwLEPaBD+9vogByz6Wrun6DoHRwcf2/7pBPYemtvI8w7w+uXq8y8BsIV5hsZXkvOx62w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NXPnEkwskvcjHatt/wGA1mF/6cLlOH8VzEpCGD/2fDRdS93zOdrs2F5Z0O08B0zEm99RNpjq1kpmxUFSauAIbg==')})
  }

        $('bookCover_25358242').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_25358242').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_25358242').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
